namespace = former_triggered_modifiers

character_event = {
	id = former_triggered_modifiers.1
	hide_window = yes
	
	only_rulers = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = defend_minor
		}
		independent = yes
		any_war = {
			defender = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = defend_minor
			days = -1
		}
		set_character_flag = defend_minor
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = former_triggered_modifiers.2
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_character_flag = defend_minor
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_ruler = no
			independent = no
			NOT = {
				any_war = {
					defender = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		remove_character_modifier = defend_minor
		clr_character_flag = defend_minor
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = former_triggered_modifiers.37
	hide_window = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	only_capable = yes
	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_character_flag = ruler_command_no
			is_republic = yes
			is_theocracy = yes
		}
		independent = yes
		war = yes
		in_command = no
		OR = {
			is_female = no
			AND = {
				is_pregnant = no
				OR = {
					feminist_religions_trigger = yes
					primary_title = {
						OR = {
							has_law = status_of_women_3
							has_law = status_of_women_4
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = ruler_command_no
			days = -1
		}
		set_character_flag = ruler_command_no
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = former_triggered_modifiers.38
	hide_window = yes
	has_character_flag = ruler_command_no
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_republic = yes
			is_theocracy = yes
			independent = no
			is_ruler = no
			war = no
			in_command = yes
			AND = {
				is_female = yes
				OR = {
					is_pregnant = yes
					feminist_religions_trigger = no
					primary_title = {
						NOR = {
							has_law = status_of_women_3
							has_law = status_of_women_4
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		remove_character_modifier = ruler_command_no
		clr_character_flag = ruler_command_no
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = former_triggered_modifiers.39
	hide_window = yes
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	trigger = {
		independent = yes
		OR = {
			is_feudal = yes
			is_tribal = yes
			is_nomadic = yes
		}
		NOR = {
			has_character_flag = weak_diplomacy
			diplomacy = 5
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = weak_diplomacy
			days = -1
		}
		set_character_flag = weak_diplomacy
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = former_triggered_modifiers.181
	hide_window = yes
	only_playable = yes
	religion = adoptionist
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = ruler_adoptionist
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = ruler_adoptionist
			days = -1
		}
		set_character_flag = ruler_adoptionist
	}
}

	hide_window = yes
	only_playable = yes
	religion = maher
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = ruler_maher
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = ruler_maher
			days = -1
		}
		set_character_flag = ruler_maher
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = former_triggered_modifiers.364
	hide_window = yes
	has_character_flag = ruler_maher
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_playable = no
			is_landed = no
			NOT = {
				religion = maher	
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		remove_character_modifier = ruler_maher
		clr_character_flag = ruler_maher
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = former_triggered_modifiers.408
	hide_window = yes
	has_character_flag = ruler_monophysite
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_playable = no
			is_landed = no
			NOT = {
				religion = monophysite	
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		remove_character_modifier = ruler_monophysite
		clr_character_flag = ruler_monophysite
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = former_triggered_modifiers.409
	hide_window = yes
	only_playable = yes
	religion = monothelite
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = ruler_monothelite
		}
	}

		days = 1

	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = ruler_monothelite
			days = -1
		}
		set_character_flag = ruler_monothelite
	}
}
